Allocates a new \doxylink{structShVkPipelinePool}{Sh\+Vk\+Pipeline\+Pool} structure. 

This macro allocates heap memory for a new \doxylink{structShVkPipelinePool}{Sh\+Vk\+Pipeline\+Pool} structure and initializes it to zero.

\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
Pointer to the newly allocated \doxylink{structShVkPipelinePool}{Sh\+Vk\+Pipeline\+Pool} structure, or NULL if allocation fails. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\Hypertarget{shVulkan_8h_a4df49a295649705c30fe92316487464b}\index{shVulkan.h@{shVulkan.h}!shVkError@{shVkError}}
\index{shVkError@{shVkError}!shVulkan.h@{shVulkan.h}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{shVulkan_8h_a4df49a295649705c30fe92316487464b} 
\#define sh\+Vk\+Error(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{condition}{, }\item[{}]{error\+\_\+msg}{, }\item[{}]{failure\+\_\+expression}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ ((\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})(condition))\ \{\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ printf(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}shvulkan\ error:\ \%s\(\backslash\)n"{}},\ (\textcolor{keyword}{const}\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*)(error\_msg));\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ failure\_expression;\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}


Error-\/checking macro for Vulkan conditions. 

This macro checks a given condition. If the condition evaluates to true, it prints an error message and executes a failure expression (like returning from a function or exiting).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em condition} & The condition to check (non-\/zero for an error). \\
\hline
{\em error\+\_\+msg} & A message to be printed if the condition is true. \\
\hline
{\em failure\+\_\+expression} & The expression to execute when the condition is true (e.\+g., return or exit).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This macro does not return any value but executes the failure\+\_\+expression if the condition is met. 
\end{DoxyNote}
\Hypertarget{shVulkan_8h_a7fef53e61a3d62b029fe8746f3628dce}\index{shVulkan.h@{shVulkan.h}!shVkResultError@{shVkResultError}}
\index{shVkResultError@{shVkResultError}!shVulkan.h@{shVulkan.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{shVkResultError}{shVkResultError}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{shVulkan_8h_a7fef53e61a3d62b029fe8746f3628dce} 
\#define sh\+Vk\+Result\+Error(\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{}]{result}{, }\item[{}]{error\+\_\+msg}{, }\item[{}]{failure\+\_\+expression}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

{\bfseries Value\+:}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{if}\ ((VkResult)(result)\ !=\ VK\_SUCCESS)\ \{\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ printf(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}shvulkan\ error:\ \%s,\ \%s\(\backslash\)n"{}},\ error\_msg,\ \mbox{\hyperlink{shVulkan_8h_ab10f609829185e735e0612e8c2a23445}{shTranslateVkResult}}((VkResult)(result)));\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ failure\_expression;\(\backslash\)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \}}

\end{DoxyCode}


Error-\/checking macro for Vulkan Vk\+Result. 

This macro checks the result of a Vulkan API call. If the result is not VK\+\_\+\+SUCCESS, it prints an error message along with the translated Vulkan error code and executes a failure expression (like returning from a function or exiting).


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em result} & The Vk\+Result from a Vulkan function (VK\+\_\+\+SUCCESS or an error code). \\
\hline
{\em error\+\_\+msg} & A message to be printed if the result is not VK\+\_\+\+SUCCESS. \\
\hline
{\em failure\+\_\+expression} & The expression to execute when the result is an error (e.\+g., return or exit).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This macro calls {\ttfamily \doxylink{shVulkan_8h_ab10f609829185e735e0612e8c2a23445}{sh\+Translate\+Vk\+Result()}} to convert the Vk\+Result enum into a string representation. 
\end{DoxyNote}

typedef struct Sh\+Vk\+Pipeline Sh\+Vk\+Pipeline}



Structure representing a Vulkan pipeline. 

This structure holds all the necessary state and configuration for creating and managing a Vulkan pipeline. \Hypertarget{shVulkan_8h_a50e29521dee75adcd4c4007570df5103}\index{shVulkan.h@{shVulkan.h}!ShVkPipelinePool@{ShVkPipelinePool}}
\index{ShVkPipelinePool@{ShVkPipelinePool}!shVulkan.h@{shVulkan.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{ShVkPipelinePool}{ShVkPipelinePool}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{shVulkan_8h_a50e29521dee75adcd4c4007570df5103} 
typedef struct Sh\+Vk\+Pipeline\+Pool Sh\+Vk\+Pipeline\+Pool}



Represents a collection of Vulkan pipeline objects and their related resources. 

This structure holds arrays of Vulkan pipelines, descriptor set layouts, descriptor pools, and other related resources required to manage and use Vulkan pipelines in a pipeline pool.

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{shVulkan_8h_a3d82b550f662b158986c904a1c6da096} 
uint8\+\_\+t sh\+Acquire\+Swapchain\+Image (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Vk\+Device}]{device}{, }\item[{Vk\+Swapchain\+KHR}]{swapchain}{, }\item[{uint64\+\_\+t}]{timeout\+\_\+ns}{, }\item[{Vk\+Semaphore}]{acquired\+\_\+signal\+\_\+semaphore}{, }\item[{Vk\+Fence}]{acquired\+\_\+signal\+\_\+fence}{, }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+swapchain\+\_\+image\+\_\+index}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+swapchain\+\_\+suboptimal}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Acquires an image from the Vulkan swapchain. 

This function acquires an image from the specified swapchain and optionally signals a semaphore or fence.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em device} & Valid Vulkan device. \\
\hline
{\em swapchain} & Valid Vulkan swapchain from which to acquire an image. \\
\hline
{\em timeout\+\_\+ns} & Timeout in nanoseconds to wait for the image. \\
\hline
{\em acquired\+\_\+signal\+\_\+semaphore} & Valid Vulkan semaphore to signal upon acquisition. \\
\hline
{\em acquired\+\_\+signal\+\_\+fence} & Valid Vulkan fence to signal upon acquisition. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+swapchain\+\_\+image\+\_\+index} & Valid destination pointer to the index of the acquired swapchain image. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+swapchain\+\_\+suboptimal} & Valid destination pointer to a flag indicating if the swapchain is suboptimal.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if successful, 0 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

Creates a Vulkan framebuffer. 

This function creates a framebuffer with specified image views and dimensions for use with a render pass.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em device} & Valid Vulkan device. \\
\hline
{\em renderpass} & Valid Vulkan render pass. \\
\hline
{\em image\+\_\+view\+\_\+count} & Number of image views in the framebuffer. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+image\+\_\+views} & Valid pointer to an array of Vk\+Image\+View handles. \\
\hline
{\em x} & Width of the framebuffer. \\
\hline
{\em y} & Height of the framebuffer. \\
\hline
{\em z} & Depth of the framebuffer. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+framebuffer} & Valid destination pointer to the newly created Vk\+Framebuffer.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if successful, 0 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

{\em p\+\_\+resolve\+\_\+attachment\+\_\+reference} & Valid pointer to the resolve attachment reference. \\
\hline
{\em preserve\+\_\+attachment\+\_\+count} & Number of attachments to preserve. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+preserve\+\_\+attachments} & Valid pointer to an array of indices of attachments to preserve. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+subpass} & Valid destination pointer to the newly created Vk\+Subpass\+Description.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if successful, 0 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}
\Hypertarget{shVulkan_8h_ab5ebb51aaf4d84d3636c3e858e2cbc81}\index{shVulkan.h@{shVulkan.h}!shCreateSwapchain@{shCreateSwapchain}}
\index{shCreateSwapchain@{shCreateSwapchain}!shVulkan.h@{shVulkan.h}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{shCreateSwapchain()}{shCreateSwapchain()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{shVulkan_8h_ab5ebb51aaf4d84d3636c3e858e2cbc81} 
uint8\+\_\+t sh\+Create\+Swapchain (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Vk\+Device}]{device}{, }\item[{Vk\+Physical\+Device}]{physical\+\_\+device}{, }\item[{Vk\+Surface\+Capabilities\+KHR}]{surface\+\_\+capabilities}{, }\item[{Vk\+Surface\+KHR}]{surface}{, }\item[{Vk\+Format}]{image\+\_\+format}{, }\item[{Vk\+Format \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+image\+\_\+format}{, }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t}]{swapchain\+\_\+image\+\_\+count}{, }\item[{Vk\+Sharing\+Mode}]{image\+\_\+sharing\+\_\+mode}{, }\item[{uint8\+\_\+t}]{vsync}{, }\item[{uint32\+\_\+t \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+swapchain\+\_\+image\+\_\+count}{, }\item[{Vk\+Swapchain\+KHR \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}}]{p\+\_\+swapchain}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Creates a Vulkan swapchain. 

This function sets up a Vulkan swapchain with the specified surface, image format, and other parameters.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em device} & Valid Vulkan device. \\
\hline
{\em physical\+\_\+device} & Valid Vulkan physical device. \\
\hline
{\em surface\+\_\+capabilities} & Surface capabilities struct. \\
\hline
{\em surface} & Valid Vulkan surface. \\
\hline
{\em image\+\_\+format} & Format of the images in the swapchain. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+image\+\_\+format} & Valid destination pointer to the format of the swapchain images. \\
\hline
{\em swapchain\+\_\+image\+\_\+count} & Number of images in the swapchain. \\
\hline
{\em image\+\_\+sharing\+\_\+mode} & Sharing mode for the swapchain images. \\
\hline
{\em vsync} & Flag to enable (1) or disable (0) V-\/\+Sync. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+swapchain\+\_\+image\+\_\+count} & Valid destination pointer to the number of swapchain images. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+swapchain} & Valid destination pointer to the newly created Vk\+Swapchain\+KHR.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
p\+\_\+swapchain\+\_\+image\+\_\+count might be different from swapchain\+\_\+image\+\_\+count when swapchain\+\_\+image\+\_\+count is not supported! Please take this in consideration for your API implementations.
\end{DoxyNote}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if the swapchain is created successfully, 0 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

\hline

\hline
\end{DoxyParams}

\end{DoxyReturn}

{\em vertex\+\_\+binding\+\_\+count} & Number of vertex input bindings. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+vertex\+\_\+bindings} & Valid pointer to an array of Vulkan vertex input binding descriptions. \\
\hline
{\em vertex\+\_\+attribute\+\_\+count} & Number of vertex input attributes. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+vertex\+\_\+attributes} & Valid pointer to an array of Vulkan vertex input attribute descriptions. \\
\hline
{\em p\+\_\+vertex\+\_\+input\+\_\+state} & Valid destination pointer to the Vulkan pipeline vertex input state create info.\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
1 if successful, 0 otherwise. 
\end{DoxyReturn}

const char \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*} sh\+Translate\+Vk\+Result (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Vk\+Result}]{vk\+\_\+result}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [extern]}}



Translates a Vk\+Result enum into a literal string. 

This function converts a Vulkan {\ttfamily Vk\+Result} code into a literal string that describes the result, which is helpful for error messages and debugging.


\begin{DoxyParams}{Parameters}
{\em vk\+\_\+result} & The Vulkan result code (Vk\+Result).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyParams}
\begin{DoxyReturn}{Returns}
A string representing the Vulkan result literal.
\end{DoxyReturn}
\begin{DoxyNote}{Note}
This function is often used in error reporting to provide more descriptive information about Vulkan errors, such as converting {\ttfamily VK\+\_\+\+ERROR\+\_\+\+OUT\+\_\+\+OF\+\_\+\+HOST\+\_\+\+MEMORY} to its string form. 
\end{DoxyNote}
